<div class="subpage_title_block">
<a href="/title/tt0120338/?ref_=ttqt_qt_tt"> <img alt="Titanic (1997) Poster" class="poster" height="98" itemprop="image" src="http://ia.media-imdb.com/images/M/MV5BMjExNzM0NDM0N15BMl5BanBnXkFtZTcwMzkxOTUwNw@@._V1_SX67_CR0,0,67,98_AL_.jpg" width="67"/>
</a> <div class="parent">
<h3 itemprop="name">
<a href="/title/tt0120338/?ref_=ttqt_qt_tt" itemprop="url">Titanic</a> <span class="nobr">
             (1997)
         </span>
</h3>
</div>

<h1 class="header">Quotes</h1>
</div>
<div class="header" id="quotes_content">
<div class="header"><div class="nav"><div class="desc">Showing all 138 items</div></div></div>
<div class="list">
<div class="quote soda sodavote odd" id="qt0472146"><div class="sodatext">
<p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
I love you, Jack. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
Don't you do that, don't say your good-byes. Not yet, do you understand me? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
I'm so cold. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
Listen, Rose. You're gonna get out of here, you're gonna go on and you're gonna make lots of babies, and you're gonna watch them grow. You're gonna die an old... an old lady warm in her bed, not here, not this night. Not like this, do you understand me? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
I can't feel my body. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
Winning that ticket, Rose, was the best thing that ever happened to me... it brought me to you. And I'm thankful for that, Rose. I'm thankful. You must do me this honor. Promise me you'll survive. That you won't give up, no matter what happens, no matter how hopeless. Promise me now, Rose, and never let go of that promise. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
I promise. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
Never let go. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
I'll never let go, Jack. I'll never let go. </p></div>
<div class="did-you-know-actions">
<a class="interesting-count-text" href="?item=qt0472146"> 95 of 96 found this interesting</a>
<span class="interesting-cast-vote" data-item-id="qt0472146" data-item-type="quotes">
<span>Interesting?</span>
<button class="cast-vote" value="up">Yes</button>

</div>
</div> <div class="quote soda sodavote even" id="qt0472111"><div class="sodatext">
<p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
Don't do it. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
Stay back! Don't come any closer! </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
Come on, just give me your hand. I'll pull you back over. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
No, stay where you are! I mean it! I'll let go! </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">He approaches slowly, gesturing to his cigarette to show that he is approaching merely to throw it over the side into the ocean</span>]
No, you won't. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
What do you mean, "No, I won't"? Don't presume to tell me what I will and will not do, you don't know me! </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
Well, you woulda done it already. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
You're distracting me! Go away! </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
I can't. I'm involved now. You let go, and I'm, I'm 'onna have to jump in there after you. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
Don't be absurd. You'd be killed! </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
I'm a good swimmer. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
The fall alone would kill you. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
It would hurt. I'm not saying it wouldn't. Tell you the truth, I'm a lot more concerned about that water being so cold. </p><p>
[<span class="fine">pause. She looks down at the water. Jack is slowly removing his boots</span>]
</p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
How cold? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
Freezing. Maybe a couple degrees over. You ever, uh, you ever been to Wisconsin? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
What? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
Well, they have some of the coldest winters around. I grew up there, near Chippewa Falls. I remember when I was a kid, me and my father, we went ice fishing out on Lake Wissota. Ice fishing is, you know, where you... </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
I know what ice fishing is! </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
Sorry. You just seem like, you know, kind of an indoor girl. Anyway, I, uh, I fell through some thin ice; and I'm telling you, water that cold, like right down there... </p><p>
[<span class="fine">He gestures with his chin down toward the Atlantic Ocean</span>]
</p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
... it hits you like a thousand knives stabbing you all over your body. You can't breathe. You can't think. At least, not about anything but the pain. Which is why I'm not looking forward to jumping in there after you. </p><p>
[<span class="fine">They exchange glances</span>]
</p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
Like I said, I don't have a choice. I guess I'm kinda hoping you'll come back over the railing, an' get me off the hook here. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
You're crazy. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
That's what everybody says but, with all due respect, Miss, I'm not the one hanging off the back of a ship here. Come on. C'mon, give me your hand. You don't want to do this. </p><p>
[<span class="fine">She reaches her hand back, he reaches his forward, and he helps her back onto the deck</span>]
</p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
Whew! I'm Jack Dawson. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
Rose De Witt Bukater. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
I'm gonna have to get you to write that one down. </p></div>

<p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
Well, yes, ma'am, I do... I mean, I got everything I need right here with me. I got air in my lungs, a few blank sheets of paper. I mean, I love waking up in the morning not knowing what's gonna happen or, who I'm gonna meet, where I'm gonna wind up. Just the other night I was sleeping under a bridge and now here I am on the grandest ship in the world having champagne with you fine people. I figure life's a gift and I don't intend on wasting it. You don't know what hand you're gonna get dealt next. You learn to take life as it comes at you... to make each day count. </p></div>

</div> <div class="quote soda sodavote odd" id="qt0472173"><div class="sodatext">
<p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
Do you love him? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
Pardon me? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
Do you love him? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
Well, you're being very rude. You shouldn't be asking me this. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
Well, it's a simple question. Do you love the guy or not? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
This is not a suitable conversation. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
Why can't you just answer the question? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
This is absurd. I don't know you and you don't know me and we are not having this conversation at all. You are rude and uncouth, and presumptuous, and I am leaving now. </p><p>
[<span class="fine">starts shaking Jack's hand</span>]
</p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
Jack... Mister Dawson, it's been a pleasure. I've sought you out to thank you, and now I have thanked you. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
And even insulted me. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
Well, you deserved it. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
Right. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
Right. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">Rose is still shaking his hand</span>]
I thought you were leaving. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">turns to leave</span>]
I am. You are so annoying. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
Ha, ha. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">turns back to Jack</span>]
Wait, I don't have to leave, this is my part of the ship. You leave. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
Oh ho, ho, well well well, now who's being rude? </p></div>

<p>
<a href="/name/nm0001784/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Old Rose</span></a>:
Fifteen-hundred people went into the sea, when Titanic sank from under us. There were twenty boats floating nearby... and only one came back. One. Six were saved from the water, myself included. Six... out of fifteen-hundred. Afterward, the seven-hundred people in the boats had nothing to do but wait... wait to die... wait to live... wait for an absolution... that would never come. </p></div>

</div> <div class="quote soda sodavote odd" id="qt0472123"><div class="sodatext">
<p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
Rose, you're no picnic, all right? You're a spoiled little brat, even, but under that, you're the most amazingly, astounding, wonderful girl, woman that I've ever known... </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
Jack, I... </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
No, let me try and get this out. You're ama- I'm not an idiot, I know how the world works. I've got ten bucks in my pocket, I have no-nothing to offer you and I know that. I understand. But I'm too involved now. You jump, I jump remember? I can't turn away without knowing you'll be all right... That's all that I want. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
Well, I'm fine... I'll be fine... really. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
Really? I don't think so. They've got you trapped, Rose. And you're gonna die if you don't break free. Maybe not right away because you're strong but... sooner or later that fire that I love about you, Rose... that fire's gonna burn out... </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
It's not up to you to save me, Jack. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
You're right... only you can do that. </p></div>

</div> <div class="quote soda sodavote odd" id="qt0472160"><div class="sodatext">
<p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
Hello Jack. I changed my mind. They said you might be out here. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
Shhh. Gimme your hand. Now close your eyes, go on. Now step up. Now hold on to the railing. Keep your eyes closed, don't peek. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
I'm not. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
Step up on the railing. Hold on, hold on. Keep your eyes closed. Do you trust me? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
I trust you. </p><p>
[<span class="fine">Jack opens Rose's arms</span>]
</p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
All right. Open your eyes. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">gasp</span>]
I'm flying, Jack! </p><p>
[<span class="fine">Jack starts singing</span>]
</p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
Come, Josephine, in my flying machine, going up, she goes up, up she goes. </p><p>
[<span class="fine">they kiss</span>]
</p></div>

</div> <div class="quote soda sodavote odd" id="qt0472227"><div class="sodatext">
<p>
<a href="/name/nm0404993/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Ismay</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">Andrews enters room with crew behind him; he lays out architectural drawings on table, with Ismay behind him</span>]
Most unfortunate, captain! </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0001255/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Thomas Andrews</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">perspiring and trembling</span>]
Water... fourteen feet above the keel in ten minutes. In the forepeak, in all three holds and in the boiler room six. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0404993/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Ismay</span></a>:
When can we get underway, damnit! </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0001255/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Thomas Andrews</span></a>:
That's five compartments! She can stay afloat with the first four compartments breached, but not five! </p><p>
[<span class="fine">tersely to Smith</span>]
</p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0001255/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Thomas Andrews</span></a>:
Not five. As she goes down by the head, the water will spill over the tops of the bulkheads at E deck from one to the next. Back and back. There's no stopping it. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0384060/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Smith</span></a>:
The pumps... if we opened the doors... </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0001255/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Thomas Andrews</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">interrupting</span>]
The pumps buy you time, but minutes only. From this moment, no matter what we do, Titanic will founder. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0404993/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Ismay</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">incredulously</span>]
But this ship can't sink! </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0001255/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Thomas Andrews</span></a>:
She's made of iron, sir! I assure you, she can... and she will. It is a mathematical certainty. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0384060/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Smith</span></a>:
How much time? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0001255/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Thomas Andrews</span></a>:
An hour... two at most. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0384060/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Smith</span></a>:
And how many aboard, Mr. Murdoch? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0829380/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">1st Officer William Murdoch</span></a>:
2,200 souls on board, sir. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0384060/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Smith</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">turning to Ismay</span>]
Well, I believe you may get your headlines, Mr. Ismay. </p></div>

<p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
Teach me to ride like a man. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
And chew tobacco like a man. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
And spit like a man! </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
What, they didn't teach you that in finishing school? </p></div>

<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
No, no, that's not what I was thinking. What I was thinking was, what could've happened to this girl to make her think she had no way out? </p></div>

<p>
[<span class="fine">Rose jumps from the saving boat and goes to where Jack is</span>]
</p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
Rose! You're so stupid. Why did you do that, huh? You're so stupid, Rose. Why did you do that? Why? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
You jump, I jump, right? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
Right. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
Oh God! I couldn't go. I couldn't go, Jack. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
It's all right. We'll think of something. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
At least I'm with you. </p></div>

You unimaginable bastard! </p></div>

<a href="/name/nm0001255/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Thomas Andrews</span></a>:

Yes... I understand. </p></div>

</p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0001784/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Old Rose</span></a>:
The others were gracious and curious about the man who had saved my life. But my mother looked at him like an insect. A dangerous insect, which must be squashed quickly. </p></div>

</div> <div class="quote soda sodavote odd" id="qt0472229"><div class="sodatext">
<p>
<a href="/name/nm0008656/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Lewis Bodine</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">narrating an animated sequence of the Titanic's sinking on a TV monitor</span>]
Okay here we go. She hits the berg on the starboard side, right? She kind of bumps along punching holes like Morse code, dit dit dit, along the side, below the water line. Then the forward compartments start to flood. Now as the water level rises, it spills over the watertight bulkheads, which unfortunately don't go any higher then E deck. So now as the bow goes down, the stern rises up. Slow at first, then faster and faster until finally she's got her whole ass sticking up in the air - And that's a big ass, we're talking 20-30,000 tons. Okay? And the hull's not designed to deal with that pressure, so what happens? "KRRRRRRKKK!" She splits. Right down to the keel. And the stern falls back level. Then as the bow sinks it pulls the stern vertical and then finally detaches. Now the stern section just kind of bobs there like a cork for a couple of minutes, floods and finally goes under about 2:20am two hours and forty minutes after the collision. The bow section planes away, landing about half a mile away going about 20-30 knots when it hits the ocean floor. "BOOM, PLCCCCCGGG!"... Pretty cool, huh? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0001784/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Old Rose</span></a>:
Thank you for that fine forensic analysis, Mr. Bodine. Of course, the experience of it was... somewhat different. </p></div>

<p>
<a href="/name/nm0001784/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Old Rose</span></a>:
1,500 people went into the sea when Titanic sank from under us. There were twenty boats floating nearby, and only one came back. One. Six were saved from the water, myself included. Six, out of 1,500. Afterward, the 700 people left in the boats had nothing to do but wait... wait to die, wait to live, wait for an absolution, which would never come. </p></div>

<p>
<a href="/name/nm0000870/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Molly Brown</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">to the group who are dining at the same table</span>]
Hey, uh, who thought of the name Titanic? Was it you, Bruce? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0404993/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Ismay</span></a>:
Yes, actually. I wanted to convey sheer size, and size means stability, luxury, and above all, strength. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
Do you know of Dr. Freud, Mr. Ismay? His ideas about the male preoccupation with size might be of particular interest to you. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0004920/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Ruth</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">whispering</span>]
What's gotten into you? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
Excuse me. </p><p>
[<span class="fine">She rises and leaves</span>]
</p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0004920/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Ruth</span></a>:
I do apologize. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000870/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Molly Brown</span></a>:
She's a pistol, Cal! Hope you can handle her. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000708/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Cal Hockley</span></a>:
Well, I may have to start minding what she reads from now on, won't I, Mrs. Brown? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0404993/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Ismay</span></a>:
Freud? Who is he? Is he a passenger? </p></div>

<p>
<a href="/name/nm0143167/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Bobby Buell</span></a>:
Brock! Brock! There's a satellite call for you. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000200/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Brock Lovett</span></a>:
Bobby, we're launching now. See these submersibles going into the water? </p><p>
[<span class="fine">motions to the subs</span>]
</p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0143167/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Bobby Buell</span></a>:
Trust me, buddy, you wanna take this call. </p><p>
[<span class="fine">nods seriously as Bobby walks towards the satelitte phone</span>]
</p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000200/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Brock Lovett</span></a>:
This better be good. </p><p>
[<span class="fine">follows Bobby to the satellite phone</span>]
</p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0143167/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Bobby Buell</span></a>:
Now, ya gotta speak up, she's kinda old. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000200/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Brock Lovett</span></a>:
Great. </p><p>
[<span class="fine">picks up phone</span>]
</p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000200/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Brock Lovett</span></a>:
This is Brock Lovett. How can I help you, Mrs...? </p><p>
[<span class="fine">turns to Bobby</span>]
</p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0143167/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Bobby Buell</span></a>:
Calvert. Rose Calvert. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000200/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Brock Lovett</span></a>:
...Mrs. Calvert? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0001784/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Old Rose</span></a>:
I was just wondering if you had found the "Heart of the Ocean" yet, Mr. Lovett. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000200/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Brock Lovett</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">turns to Bobby, completely shocked</span>]
</p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0143167/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Bobby Buell</span></a>:
Told ya ya wanted to take the call. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000200/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Brock Lovett</span></a>:
All right, you have my attention, Rose. Can you tell us who the woman in the picture is? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0001784/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Old Rose</span></a>:
Oh yes, the woman in the picture is me. </p></div>

<p>
[<span class="fine">Old Rose is telling Lovett and his crew about the Titanic</span>]
</p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0001784/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Old Rose</span></a>:
It was the ship of dreams to everyone else. To me it was a slave ship, taking me back to America in chains. Outwardly, I was everything a well brought up girl should be. Inside, I was screaming. </p></div>

</p><p>

<p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">deleted scenes</span>]
I never cared too much for all that Dadaism and Cubism. Just had no heart. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
I like some of it. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
Really? For me Paris was more about living on the streets and trying to put it on paper. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
You know, my dream has always been to run away and become an artist, Living in a garrett poor but free! </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
You wouldn't last 2 days. Theres no hot water and hardly any caviar. </p></div>

<p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
You liked this woman. You used her several times. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
Well, she has beautiful hands, see? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
I think you must have had a love affair with her. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
No no no, just with her hands. </p><p>
[<span class="fine">turns page</span>]
</p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
She was a one-legged prostitute. See? Ah, she had a good sense of humour though. </p></div>

</div> <div class="quote soda sodavote even" id="qt0472222"><div class="sodatext">
<p>
<a href="/name/nm0001255/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Thomas Andrews</span></a>:
Mr. Lightoller, why are the boats being launched half full? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0680526/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Second Officer Charles Herbert Lightoller</span></a>:
Not now, Mr. Andrews. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0001255/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Thomas Andrews</span></a>:
Look, 20 or so in a boat built for 65? And I saw one boat with only 12, 12! </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0680526/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Second Officer Charles Herbert Lightoller</span></a>:
Well, we weren't sure of the weight, Mr. Andrews. These boats may buckle. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0001255/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Thomas Andrews</span></a>:
Rubbish! They were tested in Belfast with the weight of 70 men! Now, fill these boats, Mr. Lightoller, for God's sake, man! </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0680526/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Second Officer Charles Herbert Lightoller</span></a>:
Please, I need more women and children, please! </p></div>

</div> <div class="quote soda sodavote odd" id="qt0472197"><div class="sodatext">
<p>
<a href="/name/nm0008656/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Lewis Bodine</span></a>:
She's a goddamn liar! Some nutcase seeking money or publicity, God only knows what. Like that Russian babe, Anesthesia. </p><p>
[<span class="fine">Mistaken name, intentionally kept in the scene</span>]
</p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0008656/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Lewis Bodine</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">walking towards the helicopter with Bobby following behind</span>]
</p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0008656/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Lewis Bodine</span></a>:
Rose DeWitt Bukater died on the Titanic when she was seventeen, right? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000200/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Brock Lovett</span></a>:
That's right. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0008656/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Lewis Bodine</span></a>:
If she had lived, she'd be over a hundred by now. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000200/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Brock Lovett</span></a>:
One-hundred and one next month. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0008656/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Lewis Bodine</span></a>:
Okay, so she's a very OLD goddamn liar! Look, I've already done the background on this woman all the way back to the twenties, when she was working as an actress. An actress! There's your first clue, Sherlock! Her name was Rose Dawson back then. Then she marries this guy named Calvert, they move to Cedar Rapids and she punches out a couple of kids. Now Calvert's dead, and from what I hear Cedar Rapids is dead! </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000200/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Brock Lovett</span></a>:
And everyone who knows about the diamond is supposed to be dead, or on this boat, but she knows! </p></div>

<p>
<a href="/name/nm0384060/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Smith</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">rushing to the helm after the iceberg strike</span>]
What happened, Mr. Murdoch? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0829380/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">1st Officer William Murdoch</span></a>:
An iceberg, sir. I put a hard a'starboard on the engines, full astern, but it was too close. I tried to port 'round it, but she hit. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0384060/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Smith</span></a>:
Close the watertight doors. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0829380/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">1st Officer William Murdoch</span></a>:
Doors are closed, sir. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0384060/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Smith</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">walking on deck</span>]
All stop! </p><p>
[<span class="fine">to Murdoch</span>]
</p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0384060/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Smith</span></a>:
Find the carpenter. Get him to sound the ship. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0829380/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">1st Officer William Murdoch</span></a>:
Yes, sir! </p></div>

<p>
[<span class="fine">scoffs as Rose's paintings are being unpacked</span>]
</p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000708/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Cal Hockley</span></a>:
God, not those finger paintings again. They certainly were a waste of money. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
The difference between Cal's taste in art and mine is that I have some. They're fascinating. It's like being inside a dream or something. There's truth but no logic. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0301401/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Trudy Bolt</span></a>:
What's the artist's name? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
Something Picasso. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000708/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Cal Hockley</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">scoffs</span>]
Something Picasso? He won't amount to a thing. </p><p>
[<span class="fine">pause</span>]
</p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000708/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Cal Hockley</span></a>:
He won't, trust me. At least they were cheap. </p></div>

</div> <div class="quote soda sodavote even" id="qt0472114"><div class="sodatext">
<p>
<a href="/name/nm0384060/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Smith</span></a>:
Clear. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0680526/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Second Officer Charles Herbert Lightoller</span></a>:
Yes. I don't think I've ever seen such a flat calm. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0384060/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Smith</span></a>:
Like a mill pond, not a breath of wind. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0680526/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Second Officer Charles Herbert Lightoller</span></a>:
It will make the bergs harder to see... with no breaking water at the base. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0384060/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Smith</span></a>:
Hmm. Well, I'm off. Mantain speed and heading, Mr. Lightoller. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0680526/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Second Officer Charles Herbert Lightoller</span></a>:
Yes, sir. </p></div>

<p>
<a href="/name/nm0741645/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Countess of Rothes</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">coming out of her stateroom with a confused look on her face; sees a steward and stops him</span>]
Excuse me, why have the engines stopped? I felt a shudder. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0289211/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Steward #1</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">calmly</span>]
I shouldn't worry, madam. We've likely thrown a propeller blade, that's the shudder you felt. May I bring you anything? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0741645/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Countess of Rothes</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">is distracted for a moment as Thomas Andrews passes by in a nervous hurry with an armload of the ship's plans under one arm; redirecting her attention back to the steward as he disappears</span>]
No, thank you. </p></div>

<p>
<a href="/name/nm0109229/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Robert Hitchins</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">deleted scene</span>]
C'mon, pull! Pull! </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0384060/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Smith</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">Over brass megaphone</span>]
Come back! Come back to the ship! Boat 6, come back to the ship! </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000870/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Molly Brown</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">to other rowers</span>]
Stop! We have to go back! </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0109229/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Robert Hitchins</span></a>:
No. The suction will pull us down if we don't keep going. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000870/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Molly Brown</span></a>:
We've lots more room! I say we go back. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0109229/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Robert Hitchins</span></a>:
No! It's our lives now, not theirs. And I'm in charge of this boat, madam! Now *row*! </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0384060/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Smith</span></a>:
This is the captain! This is the captain! Come back! </p><p>
[<span class="fine">pause</span>]
</p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0384060/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Smith</span></a>:
The fools. </p></div>

</div> <div class="quote soda sodavote even" id="qt1681894"><div class="sodatext">
<p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
Staring up at the sky, Look. It's so beautiful. SO vast and endless. They're so small. My crowd, they think they're giants. They're not even dust in Gods eyes. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
Well, there's been a mistake. You're not one of them. You got mailed to the wrong address. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
Laughs, I did, didn't I? LOOK, a shooting star! </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
It was a long one. You know, my Pop's used to tell me, every time he saw one, it was a soul going to heaven. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
I like that. Are we supposed to wish on it? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000138/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Jack</span></a>:
Why? What would you wish for? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0000701/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Rose</span></a>:
Something I can't have. </p></div>

[<span class="fine">whispering to Jack</span>]
Now they will retreat into a cloud of smoke and congratulate each other on being masters of the universe. </p></div>

</div> <div class="quote soda sodavote odd" id="qt0472228"><div class="sodatext">
<p>
<a href="/name/nm0404993/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Ismay</span></a>:
So you've not yet lit the last four boilers? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0384060/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Smith</span></a>:
No, I don't see the need. We are making excellent time. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0404993/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Ismay</span></a>:
The press knows the size of Titanic. Now I want them to marvel at her speed. We must give them something new to print! This maiden voyage of Titanic must make headlines! </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0384060/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Smith</span></a>:
Mr. Ismay, I would prefer not to push the engines until they've been properly run in. </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0404993/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Ismay</span></a>:
Of course, I'm just a passenger. I leave it to your good offices to decide what's best. But what a glorious end to your final crossing if we were to get to New York on Tuesday night and surprise them all! Make the morning papers. Retire with a bang, eh E.J.? </p><p>
<a href="/name/nm0404993/?ref_=tt_trv_qu"><span class="character">Ismay</span></a>:
[<span class="fine">Smith nods reluctantly</span>]
Good man. </p></div>

It still gets me every time... to see the sad ruin of the great ship sitting here, where she landed at 2:30 in the morning, April 15, 1912, after her long fall from the world above. </p><p>
